 *    -----------------------------------------       *
 *        24. 8.95  C.Zeitnitz, T.A.Gabriel           *
 *                                                    *
 *     NMTC is used for hadronic interactions of      *
 *        protons,neutrons and charged pions          *
 *   up to 3.5 GeV (proton,neutron), 2.5 GeV(pion)    *
